## Diagram 2

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Application {
        +String apiVersion
        +String kind
        +Metadata metadata
        +Spec spec
    }
    class Metadata {
        +String name
        +Labels labels
    }
    class Labels {
        +String app
    }
    class Spec {
        +String project
        +Destination destination
        +Source source
        +Array sources
        +SyncPolicy syncPolicy
    }
    class Destination {
        +String name
        +String namespace
        +String server
    }
    class Source {
        +String path
        +String repoURL
        +String targetRevision
        +Helm helm
    }
    class Helm {
        +Array valueFiles
        +Array parameters
    }
    class Parameters {
        +String name
        +String value
    }
    class SyncPolicy {
        +Automated automated
    }
    class Automated {
        +Boolean prune
        +Boolean selfHeal
    }
    Application --> Metadata
    Application --> Spec
    Metadata --> Labels
    Spec --> Destination
    Spec --> Source
    Spec --> SyncPolicy
    Source --> Helm
    Helm --> Parameters
    SyncPolicy --> Automated
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> OutOfSync: Application Created
    OutOfSync --> Syncing: Automated Sync Triggered
    Syncing --> Synced: Deployment Successful
    Synced --> OutOfSync: Config Drift Detected
    OutOfSync --> Syncing: Self-Heal Enabled
    Synced --> Syncing: Updates Detected
    Syncing --> Failed: Deployment Failed
    Failed --> Syncing: Retry
    Synced --> Pruning: Resources Removed from Git
    Pruning --> Synced: Prune Successful
```
